Resolution of the Dispute Over the Head of the Fujian Finance Department 71

▲ The Anti-He Wave in the Party Subsides

A dispatch from Fuzhou states that after the appointment of He Gonggan as the new acting head of the Fujian Provincial Finance Department and special commissioner of finance was announced, two instructors from the provincial party headquarters, Gan Yun and Feng Ji'an, opposed the appointment on the grounds that He was an important figure in the State-Nationalist faction. Party branches at all levels echoed the opposition, and the city was plastered with slogans and leaflets calling for He's expulsion, creating a very serious situation. The provincial party headquarters and the provincial government telegraphed the Central Government and the National Government for instructions. However, He Gonggan himself insisted that he had no connection with the State-Nationalist faction and adopted a very firm attitude. On the morning of the 21st, amidst a pervading atmosphere of opposition, he resolutely took over the Finance Department and the Special Commissioner's Office, reorganizing the department and replacing various staff members. As previously reported, personnel holding nominal or concurrent positions were also dismissed, totaling over seventy people from both the department and the office, saving over 17,000 yuan in expenses each month. At the same time, he raised 100,000 yuan in cash from a certain source to cover current military and administrative expenses. Regarding the future direction of financial reorganization, He stated that all national and local taxes would be increased, and the amount compared to the assessment implemented through open bidding. Responsible personnel would not be allowed to privately transfer or take over operations, secretly form partnerships to share dividends, or collect subsidies. All such abuses should be vigorously eliminated to convert private gains into public benefits. According to this method, an additional 300,000 yuan could be increased each month. However, opponents were greatly shaken that He had taken office without waiting for a reply from the Central Government and decided to convene a joint meeting of various party district branches and mass organizations on the morning of the 22nd to discuss countermeasures. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 21st, Hu Hanmin, a member of the Central Committee, replied in a telegram, stating that when Chen Zhenru was retained as the deputy director of the Political Department of the Commander-in-Chief at the 91st Political Conference in May of the 16th year of the Republic, a resolution included that He Gonggan and others were recently striving for the Three Principles of the People, and their achievements were known to the Central Government. All those who cherish the late President's magnanimity and the necessity of concentrating talents in the Party should not seize floating rumors and facts, strip useful talents, and lightly attack the enemy. For this reason, the Central Political Conference believes that Comrade He and others should summon the courage to make a self-reflection, redouble their efforts in their original posts, etc. Upon receiving the inquiry, a portion of the original document was released and reported. The provincial government immediately turned the original telegram over to various newspapers for publication, so the atmosphere of the 22nd changed abruptly, and the anti-He movement suddenly subsided. The slogans and leaflets posted in the city were also cleaned up by the Public Security Bureau. In the afternoon, Yang Shuzhuang specially invited the committee members to the provincial government to talk with He Gonggan, dispel misunderstandings, and foster feelings. Gan Yun and Feng Ji'an are scheduled to take the Jiahe steamer to Shanghai on the 23rd and then to Beijing to report on the reorganization of the provincial party headquarters to the Central Government. The dispute over the head of the Fujian Finance Department, which lasted for a week, has thus come to an end. (July 23rd)

Rampant Banditry in Su County, Northern Anhui 72

A dispatch from Bengbu states that Su County in northern Anhui, located at a key point along the Jinpu Railway, is adjacent to Xiaoxian County in Jiangsu and Yongcheng County in Henan, both notoriously infested with bandits. Over the years, accumulated bandits have wreaked havoc, causing great suffering to the local population. Although repeated suppression efforts have been conducted by the military, police, and local militias, bandits return as soon as the forces leave, and the area has never been pacified. Recently, since the outbreak of the Henan War, bandits have taken advantage of the opportunity to rise again. In early May, bandits in the Dafang Temple area successively broke through many stockaded villages. They were scattered by the local police and militia forces, but in early July, bandits in the Linyu district of the county, incited by communists, rose up in succession in Houlou, Xulou, Qiianhouying, Taitousi and other places on the 7th, 8th, and 9th days, gathering two to three hundred people, robbing, looting, burning, and killing in an extremely rampant manner. The district sent the first and second teams of the People's Self-Defense Corps to Zoulou, Youzha and other places in the northwest to block and defend, while the head of the local militia personally led troops to Houlou to cooperate with the Baishan district self-defense corps to jointly suppress the bandits. The bandits were repelled at Xiangshuibiao and Yeliuhu, and were then pursued to Taitousi before they were scattered. Not long after, six to seven hundred fierce bandits from Yongcheng in eastern Henan infiltrated the Baishan district, occupied Cheji in the northwest of the district, and became very rampant. On the 22nd, Zhao, the head of the Baishan district militia, reported to the county, and County Magistrate Wei Zhanyuan ordered the headquarters of the County People's Self-Defense Corps to immediately summon the self-defense corps from each district to jointly suppress the bandits. The headquarters of the county militia immediately mobilized the self-defense corps from the five southern districts and the mortar team from Jishi Village to launch a vigorous suppression. The county garrison also sent Shao, the platoon leader of the second battalion, to lead the self-defense corps from Baishan, Linyu and other districts to meet and attack the bandits. The bandits engaged in a fierce battle with the militia on the 23rd in Wenzhuang and Xiaozhouzhuang of Liuguji, located on the border of Baishan and Suixi. The bandits were overwhelmed and collapsed. Platoon Leader Shao did not pursue them due to limited ammunition. Several soldiers were injured or killed in this battle. The county garrison and the self-defense corps from each district are adopting a joint encirclement strategy to annihilate the bandits as soon as possible. (July 26th)

Pre-Decision Points for the Civil Code's Sections on Inheritance and Kinship 73

Review Opinions of the Central Political Council

Hu Hanmin, President of the Legislative Yuan, and Lin Sen, Vice President, previously submitted several points that should be decided first regarding the Civil Code's sections on Inheritance and Kinship to the Central Political Council. The Central Political Council handed them over to the Legal Affairs Group for review, and they were revised and passed in accordance with the review opinions at the 236th meeting. The review opinion document is extracted as follows:

(1) Points to be decided first in Inheritance Law: First point: Should the inheritance of the lineage be stipulated? The inheritance of the lineage need not be stipulated. (Explanation) The system of lineage inheritance is detailed in the Rites of Zhou and is a relic of the feudal era. There is a distinction between the major lineage and the minor lineage. The temple of the major lineage, which does not move for a hundred generations, is called the lineage. The temple of the minor lineage, which moves after five generations, is called the ancestral shrine. This is the original meaning of the two characters lineage and shrine. The major lineage presides over the ancestral temple sacrifices and cannot be without an heir. Therefore, the minor lineage can be extinguished, but the major lineage cannot be extinguished. This is where the system of establishing an heir comes from. Since the abolition of feudalism and the demise of the clan system, the organization of society is based on the family, not the clan. Each family presides over the ancestral sacrifices and is not unified. Those who have joint family sacrifices are presided over by the clan head, not necessarily the heir of the lineage. The system of lineage head presiding over sacrifices has not been abolished, but the names of major and minor lineages have no place to attach, and the saying of establishing an heir for the major lineage has long been a false term. This is the first reason why lineage inheritance has no reason to continue to exist in terms of the system. According to old regulations, both the eldest and second sons should establish heirs. What is called the eldest son today may not belong entirely to the major lineage, let alone the second son. Moreover, among close relatives of the same father, there is the practice of adopting two lineages at the same time. As a result, the son of the eldest son may also be the heir of the second son, which is contrary to the ancient meaning of the minor lineage being extinguished. It only retains the name without the substance. This is the second reason why lineage inheritance has no reason to continue to exist in name. Lineage inheritance focuses on sacrifices, so those who establish an heir are limited to men, and women have no right to establish an heir. Those who are adopted as heirs are also limited to men, and women have no right to be an heir. The emphasis on men and the contempt for women can be seen here, which is clearly incompatible with modern trends. This is the third reason why lineage inheritance has no reason to continue to exist in terms of gender equality. Based on the above reasons, it is believed that lineage inheritance need not be stipulated. As for the selection of an heir, it is originally the freedom of the parties concerned and should not be prohibited. It should be that both men and women can select and be selected as heirs. Second point: Is inheritance of property premised on inheritance of the lineage? Inheritance of property is not premised on inheritance of the lineage. (Explanation) According to the old laws of our country, the inheritance of property is limited to men in the direct line of descent, because it is based on the inheritance of the lineage. Therefore, those who have no sons must adopt an heir from the same clan of the same generation. As a result, daughters, even if they are close, and wives who remain faithful, are not allowed to inherit property. Even though a wife who remains faithful may temporarily inherit her husband's share, she still needs to rely on the clan head to establish an heir. All of these unequal systems between men and women are now known to be unworkable. As for direct ascendants, because the old laws prohibited children and grandchildren from having separate property, ascendants would not have property to inherit if their children and grandchildren were alive. But now the situation has changed, and the prohibition of private property of the young has gradually been abolished. If they die without descendants, it would be unreasonable to establish an heir to inherit the property without allowing the parents or grandparents to have this right. Therefore, in today's situation, inheritance of property should not be premised on lineage inheritance. Third point: The scope and order of heirs, and the shares to be inherited. (1) Heirs are divided into two types: legal heirs and designated heirs. (2) Legal heirs, in addition to the spouse, are determined in the following order: (1) Direct descendants; (2) Parents; (3) Siblings; (4) Grandparents. (3) Children born out of wedlock who have been raised or recognized shall have the same rights as children born in wedlock in inheriting property. (4) Among legal heirs in the first order, regardless of gender, those with closer kinship take precedence. (5) If a legal heir in the first order dies or loses the right of inheritance before the inheritance begins, their direct descendants shall inherit their share. (6) When there is more than one legal heir, they shall inherit equally regardless of gender, unless otherwise specified. (7) The order of inheritance for adopted children is the same as for natural children, but their share of inheritance is one-half that of natural children. (8) In the absence of direct descendants, a designated heir may be appointed for all or part of the property. (9) Both the designator and the designee are not restricted by gender. (Explanation) According to the old laws of our country, the inheritance of property is limited to men in the direct line of descent. This adheres to the saying of lineage inheritance and takes the inheritance of the lineage as a prerequisite for the inheritance of property. Therefore, those who have no sons must adopt someone from the same clan who is of the same generation. Upon further investigation, even parents, grandparents, and siblings, and even children who remain at birth, cannot participate in the inheritance, which goes against human nature. Apart from the right of women to inherit property, which has already been decided by the Second National Congress and should be incorporated into the principles, it is specially stipulated that other relatives in addition to direct descendants can also be heirs in order to conform to the current trend. The scope and order of other heirs (details of the spouse are different) determined by various countries outside of direct descendants are not consistent. The following is a brief description of the heirs outside of direct descendants and spouses: Germany stipulates that parents and their descendants, grandparents and their descendants, great-grandparents and their descendants, and remote ancestors and their descendants are all legal heirs, and among them, the order is that parents and their descendants take precedence, followed by grandparents and their descendants, and so on. Switzerland stipulates that parents (those who died before are represented by their direct descendants) and grandparents (those who died before are represented by their direct descendants) are all legal heirs, and among them, the order is that parents take precedence. Brazil stipulates that direct ascendants and collateral relatives within six degrees of kinship (whether those who died before can be represented by their descendants is specified in detail) are all heirs, and among them, the order is that direct ascendants take precedence. Japan stipulates that direct ascendants are heirs, and the order is that those with closer kinship take precedence. Moreover, after direct ascendants, the head of the household is also included. Soviet Russia limits the heirs to those who have been supported by the deceased for more than one year before their death and who have no ability to work and property. Examples like these are too numerous to mention. It is now planned to assess our country's national conditions and refer to foreign precedents to allow parents, siblings, and grandparents to inherit property. (To be continued)

Local Dispatches

Jiading 74

Baby Oil Incidents: Jin Chengyong, director of the Yucheng Infant Hall, and others recently heard that babies in the hall were being fraudulently adopted by criminals for sale to Shanghai to be boiled into Yu Shu Shen oil and other medicines. They were greatly angered. In addition to thoroughly checking the records of the households who adopted babies, they also ordered the detective team to secretly investigate. It has now been found that a certain person in Shanghai has set up an organization in Yu Shouyi's house on West Main Street in the city, secretly ordering local women to go to the hall to adopt babies, paying 12 to 18 yuan per baby. They are secretly transported to Shanghai, and it has been found on the adoption certificates that Shi Wenxiu's printing shop has acted as a guarantor for five people in one day. The babies adopted by Pu Aixue and Gu Achun outside the South Gate are all missing. Pu and others were arrested. According to their confessions, the babies had either died or been fostered in Shanghai. Apart from sending the suspect for further investigation, they are also secretly arresting the fugitives for investigation.

Suzhou 75

Collapse of Buildings on Guanqian Street Injures People: Guanqian Street is now being actively widened, and shops are being demolished and rebuilt. At around 3:00 PM yesterday (the 28th), when the Qiantai Xiang Silk Store at the Zhenshanmen entrance was being demolished, it suddenly collapsed, injuring five male and female workers on the spot. The foreman hired a car to send them to Tongren Hospital on Gongyuan Road for treatment. In addition, the reconstruction of the Jinxingguan Restaurant at No. 68 Tianhougong Bridge Street inside Pingmen was sloppy last winter. At 5:00 PM yesterday (the 27th), the Jinxingguan Restaurant building suddenly collapsed, simultaneously collapsing nine neighboring shops, including Zhang Laosi's tofu shop, Yang Maotou's noodle shop, Jiang Jinfang's candy shop, a certain family's flatbread shop, He Laoqi's wonton shop, Shunhelou Restaurant, Diao Si's residence, and Zhang Laosi's tofu shop warehouse, totaling thirty rooms.

A Large Prison to be Built in Zhenru: Since the Shanghai Public Concession Provisional Court was reorganized into the Higher Second Branch Court by the Ministry of Justice on April 1st of this year, the West Prison, Women's Prison, Detention Center, and Civil Custody Office, where male and female criminal offenders were detained by the former Provisional Court, have been managed by two Western prison directors and deputy directors. Although the Ministry of Justice has been eager to recover the management to Chinese, the Concession authorities have refused, so it has not been recovered yet. However, the Ministry of Justice is determined to find a way to recover the Concession prisons, so it recently appointed Xie Fuzi, the prison director of the Third Jiangsu Prison, to Shanghai to prepare for the takeover. After Xie was commissioned, he first investigated the total number of prisoners and the financial situation. It was estimated that there were about 4,700 Chinese criminals and more than 700 foreigners detained in the West Prison. There were more than 170 female prisoners in the Women's Prison, and more than 50 civil custody prisoners. There were dozens of untried prisoners in the Detention Center. As for economic issues, it was estimated that the average cost for each Chinese criminal detained in the West Prison was about 150 taels of silver per year, and the average cost for each foreign criminal was about 2.5 yuan of silver per day. The above expenses were entirely paid by Chinese taxpayers. The costs for the female prisoners, untried prisoners, and civil custody prisoners were also higher than those in Jiangsu Province prisons. After Xie's investigation, he consulted with the president of the Higher Second Branch Court and the police on the takeover methods. After much discussion, it was only agreed to transfer the Detention Center, Women's Prison, and Civil Custody Office to Chinese management. Xie Prison Director then first took over the Detention Center and reported to the Ministry of Justice. After the Ministry of Justice received the report, it decided to find a solution because the West Prison could not be recovered and managed independently. It was decided to allocate more than 400,000 yuan of surplus funds that the Higher Second Branch Court received when the Provisional Court was transferred but had not yet used to purchase 150 to 160 acres of land in Zhenru, west of Shanghai, to build a large prison that could accommodate 3,000 prisoners to detain the tried and untried prisoners of the Special Zone Local Court in the future. Xie Fuzi has been commissioned to design the prison. After Xie was commissioned, he has been looking for suitable land. Once it is purchased, the perimeter wall will be built first, and the plan is to build in four phases. The first phase will be to build a place to accommodate 700 prisoners. Once it is satisfactory, construction will continue in succession.

Wuxi 76

The Su-Xi Water Police jointly suppressed the lake bandits who hijacked the ships at Wangyewan near Hengjing in the Su area on the 23rd. The gang of lake bandits from Henan, Pudong, and Jiangbei hijacked the "Dalu Flying Tiger" passenger ships, kidnapped Wang Wusheng, the captain of the 8th team of the 2nd Water Police District, and Inspector Huang, killed two guards, seized more than a dozen guns, and kidnapped twenty-five male and female passengers. After receiving the report, Mao Mujun, the chief of the 2nd Water Police District, immediately led the police to Hengjing. The day before yesterday, he and Gong Guoliang, the chief of the 3rd District, convened an emergency meeting of all the teams under their jurisdiction to discuss the methods of suppression. They immediately set off separately. Yesterday morning, all the police teams arrived at Dongshan, including four shallow-water warships, more than seventy patrol boats from the 2nd and 3rd Districts, and Du Hongyi, the captain of the Wuxian Police Brigade, also led two police companies together with the Water Police Guerrilla Team, and fifty patrol boats also arrived at the same time. Mao and Gong, the two district chiefs, ordered an immediate suppression to completely eliminate them. The leader of the lake bandits, Zhong Zhaokui, after hijacking at Wangyewan, fled to West Taihu with the remaining bandits and joined forces with Wang Zhongyi, Peng Qingshan, Wang Rong and other bandits to strengthen their forces. After receiving the information, the 3rd District of Zhejiang Water Police immediately sent two detectives, Wu Rongshan and Zhang Zhi, to Caogang, Su Province, on the 26th to investigate. They encountered the bandits and were killed. The Zhejiang Water Police have now sent a team to Caogang to suppress them. Salt police and smugglers fought fiercely. Recently, a gang of salt smugglers from Pudong smuggled more than ninety loads of illegal salt from overseas, loaded them on three boats, and sailed from Yangcheng Lake into Taihu Lake to sell them to villages along the lake. On the 24th, at Zhifangquan in the Xi area, Dai Shoushan, the captain of the 7th Anti-smuggling Brigade of the Su Five Districts stationed there, went to pursue them and telegraphed the 7th Brigade Headquarters in the city. Wu Hanzhuang, the brigade commander, immediately sent Huang Songyuan, the deputy captain of the 3rd Company, to lead eight patrol boats to Southern Spring to join the commercial patrol team to pursue the bandits in the lake. The two sides opened fire at Renzigang. The bandits' weapons were extremely sophisticated, all Mauser pistols. After an hour of fierce fighting, several bandits were killed. The bandits retreated to the east and west mountains. The police team was unable to pursue them due to the small boats and big waves. Yesterday, the situation was reported to the brigade headquarters for verification and decision. Chengsha merchants strived for the abolition of the public office donation. Most of the Jiangyin cotton yarn industry purchased cotton yarn from factories in Wuxi. The Wuxi Yarn Industry Guild used to collect a public office donation of one corner for each piece of yarn transported to Cheng. After Jiangyin yarn merchants strived for it, the public office donation was stopped in the 14th year of the Republic of China and changed to collecting one corner for each piece of yarn leaving the warehouse. However, the invoice still has the public office donation stamp. The yarn industry in the county sent a letter to the Jiangyin Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce for negotiation, and requested the Construction Department to order it to be stopped. After a year, it has not been resolved. The Wuxi County Government received an order from the Construction Department the day before yesterday to immediately convene the chambers of commerce of the two counties of Xi and Cheng to discuss it together and wait for a reply. County Magistrate Sun took the order and has forwarded it for notification and scheduled a meeting.

A factory apprentice was electrocuted to death. Shen Jingeng, a foundry apprentice at the Xiexin Machinery Foundry on Dongxin Road outside Guangfu Gate, Wuyi County (from Changzhou, 15 years old), was restless and unable to sleep at 4 o'clock in the morning yesterday because of bedbugs. He moved an electric lamp to catch the bedbugs. The insulation of the electric lamp wire was broken, and he was electrocuted and died immediately. The factory notified the deceased's father to come to Xi for coffining.

The dispute over corruption in the Silk Factory Engine Room Workers' Union in Xi County. Wang Xingbei, an employee of the Silk Factory Engine Room Workers' Union Engine Room Department (also known as Wu), and Xie Bin, a member of the executive committee of the union, have been illegally engaging in corruption since taking office, causing disputes. Recently, the Engine Room Department discovered 105 blank membership certificates and nine seals of various industry unions that they had privately made. These were submitted to the Industrial and Commercial Union as evidence of the employees Wu Xingbei and others engaging in private corruption. Zhang Chuncao, Gu Chengyou, Wang Rugao, and other members of the organizing committee of the Engine Room Factory Workers' Union, yesterday submitted a petition to the County Party Consolidation Committee and the People's Training Committee, requesting that a letter be sent to the County Government ordering Wang Xingbei and Xie Bin to be brought to justice for questioning and prosecution in accordance with the law to punish evil and transform evil.

Robbery, kidnapping and arson in Dongji Township. Huai'an's handling of detained wheat. The Huai'an County Government has not yet resolved the issue of detaining many boats of wheat passing through the county. County Magistrate Wang Zhenyu convened the Party Department, Li Leyao, and the district chiefs, Song Kun, to discuss everything. The resolution was recorded as follows: (1) For wheat detained in the county that is transported out of the county and cannot prove that it is not leaked from the province to the sea, the wheat merchants shall be responsible for selling it to local merchants in the county. (2) The previous high-quality wheat was about seven yuan per stone, and now it is sold for eight yuan. The second-quality wheat was six yuan, and now it is sold for seven yuan. All public sale interest should be deducted from the remaining profit of each stone by five corners and handed over to the property office for storage for relief purposes. (3) All ship owners who transport wheat out of the county shall obtain a certificate from the county government and mutually guarantee that there will be no more incidents of transporting goods outside the county. (4) The Party, government, commercial and district shall conduct inspections at any time to avoid smuggling. (5) The above cases shall be sent by the county government to the Chamber of Commerce to inform the wheat merchants to comply.

Education News Sports

The Chinese Expedition Football Team Suffered a Crushing Defeat 87

Lost to the Singapore Team by a Score of Three to Zero

丨More than 10,000 Spectators Cheered in Unison丨

(Singapore Communication, July 16)

The Chinese Expedition Football Team, which is famous throughout the country, has been retained by the local Football Association for a competition while en route to various countries in Europe and America. The competition schedule began the day before yesterday (the 13th) with a match against the Malayan Chinese United Team, which the team won. The score was two to one. Who knew that on the 16th, they would suffer a crushing defeat against the Singapore Football Team? This was truly beyond the expectations of more than 10,000 spectators, and even the team's athletes had never experienced it before. This kind of injury is no small matter and should never be forgotten. However, this matter is not entirely related to the team's own honor or disgrace. Since the team comes from the motherland, it also has a great relationship with the reputation of overseas Chinese. If they were to lose to the overseas Chinese United Team today, the matter would be insignificant. Since they are compatriots, it is not necessary to judge success or failure. But if they lose to the Singaporean teams of various colors, the matter cannot be regarded in the same light. It is found that five of the eleven team members of the Singapore team are natives, three are Europeans, and the Chinese account for the fewest. The minority team members have always had a very good reputation, and there is a hope of winning nine out of ten expeditions. The spectators at the scene all said that if the Malay team members played in today's game, they would definitely see a spectacle. The few Chinese team members present did not take it seriously. If the team could have worked together yesterday, put aside arrogance, considered their own reputation, and won glory for the overseas Chinese, then the Malay athletes would naturally not be able to shake the southern islands, and the Chinese spectators at the stadium would not have lost heart and left the stadium before the end of the game. Although failure is commonplace in military affairs, in my opinion, there are also different types of football matches: one is a crushing defeat, and the other is a narrow defeat. What is a crushing defeat? It means suffering a complete defeat and returning empty-handed. But a narrow defeat is different. It is just a defeat caused by a difference in the number of points. The team's defeat today is one of the crushing defeats and must be remedied. A Western proverb says, "Failure is the mother of success." The days ahead are long and the future is unlimited. May the team's athletes work hard and swear to avenge their previous shame. If you want to achieve this goal, you must start with the individual, first get rid of arrogance and don't have the idea that there is no one in your eyes, and then seek to unite the entire team and work together to succeed. If this is the case, then not only can you win if you advance, but you will not suffer a crushing defeat even if you retreat. I urge the Chinese team members to endure the pain and record the course of today's Chinese team's match against the Singaporean team as follows:

First Half丨One to Zero 88

The location of today's game is at the Anson Road Stadium. At around 5:02, referee Strode blew the silver whistle and summoned the two armies to prepare for battle. The circle occupied by the Singapore team was in the south of the field, while the Chinese team occupied the north of the field. After the two teams deployed their formations, the Singapore team kicked off first. The team's forward rushed forward to meet the enemy ship, and then the team encountered a corner kick, so they planned to attack. When the ball was passed to the front of the enemy's goal, they shot, but unfortunately the shot was too high and passed over the circle gate. A few seconds later, the Singapore team was penalized a ball. The Chinese kicker shot quickly, but the team members were in a hurry and the ball went out of bounds. At this time, the Chinese team's athletes were full of energy, while the Singapore team could only adopt a conservative strategy to strengthen the city gate. Then the team took the opportunity to break through the enemy's momentum like a bamboo, and was blocked three times in the enemy's goal. Although Mr. Li Huitang used his famous strange foot to shoot, he failed to enter the goal because his shot was too slow and lacked courage. His ball skills were quite different from before. If Mr. Li could be as strong as before, I believe he could have won two goals in a few minutes. But unfortunately, the ball was not shot accurately, and the Singapore team launched a counterattack. The center forward shot the ball, but it was hateful that he was in a foreign land and could not stand firm. The shot was either too high over the door or crossed the side of the door. After the two teams competed with each other, they both tended to defend first and attack later. When the team attacked, they were blocked by the Malay of the Singapore team, and the forward did not get his wish. However, the Singapore team saw that the situation was not good and planned to counterattack, but unfortunately it was blocked and a corner kick was taken again. After the ball was kicked, two athletes of the Singapore team, Mr. Yahui, tried their best to attack. Although they suffered all kinds of setbacks, their ambition was still undiminished, and the opponent could not do anything about it. However, the right wing of the team was also extremely noisy and could not come forward to show their skills against the enemy. At this time, the ball skills were quite impressive. Before long, the team's athletes rushed forward one after another to attack. Several shots were unfortunately too high and all crossed the enemy's goal. At 5:20, the Singapore team counterattacked and the center forward, a Malay athlete, shot one point and first opened the game record, and then the ceasefire was announced.

Second Half丨Two to Zero 89

After the two team members rested briefly, they changed positions and then continued the game. The Chinese team kicked off first to challenge, and after the Singapore team's forward defended, they launched an attack. Unexpectedly, the shot was blocked and the center forward used the same method to attack, but it was also blocked. After that, the forwards of the two teams began to circle and fight in the stadium. At this time, the right forward of the team took the opportunity to break through the enemy and pass the ball to the forward, but although Li Huitang had a good opportunity to shoot the ball, he still could not push the ball into the circle. However, the spectators in the stadium were greatly surprised by the Singapore team. After the corner kick, Mr. Li Huitang worked hard, but the opponent's military strength was strong and he could not easily pass the barrier. After the Singapore team counterattacked, Mr. Wenxun rushed forward and shot one point. At that time, the audience cheered and cheered for the victory of the Singapore team. At about 5:55, the Singapore team scored another goal. After that, the two teams did not make much progress, so there were no more points added. At about 6 o'clock, a big battle was declared over, and the Singapore team won the whole victory with a score of three to zero.

Two team line 90

Chinese team Zhou Xianyan Li Ning Feng Yunyou Chen Zhenhe Sun Sijing An Yuansheng Chen Guangyao Li Huitang Dai Linjing Chen Jiaqiu Cao Guicheng Singapore team Jiu Yarasha Silidu Na Yao Yadlie Min Hong Ya Wadu La Luohua Mawa

Overview of ball skills 91

Looking at today's battle, Cao Guicheng was hasty in his actions in the first half and his shots were inaccurate. In the second half, Li Huitang was slow in his movements and his shots were weak. This was the main reason for the defeat. The Singapore team knew that Zhou Xianyan was good at saving low balls, but he often lost his position due to panic when he encountered the team ball, so the shot often took advantage of the opportunity to enter. This was also a great factor in gaining victory in strategy. Although this disastrous defeat cannot be used to judge people, the laxity of the ball technique performance did disappoint the spectators. Failure is the mother of success. I hope the Lehua athletes will not be arrogant or discouraged, and they will train hard. On the one hand, they will recruit talents and cooperate sincerely. If Yao and Ya Jiu, who played in today's game, are also good players in the expedition to Europe and America, and they can be persuaded to travel with them, the strength of the expeditionary force will increase a lot. This expedition is related to the national honor and is not just a matter of Lehua team.

France Retains Davis Cup 92

Four to One ... Defeats the United States

丨Result of the Third Day's Competition: France Wins Two More Singles丨

(Paris Telegraph, 27) France, with a score of four to one, defeated its strong rival, the United States, in the 1930 Davis Cup Championship and continued to hold the championship for another year. The good news spread everywhere and the whole country was ecstatic. French President Domergue, who personally led the expedition, also stood up and cheered with the audience, happy and excited, which cannot be described in words. Even the defeated American players approached and congratulated them with their chivalrous spirit. At this moment, as the setting sun sets and the twilight is vast, the three musketeers of the Davis Cup, which shook the world and won glory for the country, declared success and slowly closed the curtain.

The Success of the Three Musketeers of France 93

France relied on the four horsemen who dominated the world of tennis for several years. This year, La Assid left the game and lived in seclusion, so the four horsemen became the three musketeers. The so-called three musketeers are Kochland, Bo Rope Latot, and White Ronny. The three musketeers in the final scene of this session have made the most of their skills, and Kochland's three-day winning record is particularly outstanding, and he deserves to be the world's number one. The ambitious American players received the heavy task of unanimous expectation from their motherland. At that time, they were exhausted and could not show anything, so they had to bow down to the rackets of the three musketeers. They only hoped to see you again next year to relieve the pain and shame of four consecutive failures.

The Course of the French and American Championships 94

On the first day of the American and French championships, both sides won a group each, which was originally expected by the audience. The doubles competition was held the next day. According to the recent strength of both sides, the United States was more confident, but in fact France was superior everywhere and finally won, leading with two to one. People already knew that this championship must be saved by France, because the last two singles groups were not illegal opponents for the United States. Sure enough, in the first game today, French Bolo Tala defeated American George Lord with a score of five to seven, six to three, two to six, six to two, and eight to six. Therefore, France's victory was set, and Kochland's victory over American Tierden with a score of three to one can also be regarded as a performance competition and has nothing to do with the overall situation. As a result, France won the championship with a score of four to one and continued to hold it for another year.

Lord Suffers Hard Loss 95

The defeat of French Bolo Tala by American Lord was hopeless, but his record that day was exceptionally good, more stable and more skillful than when he competed with Kochland. The performance of French Bolo Tala can be called a model. The best points are splitting and intercepting, which almost made the Americans exhausted. In the fifth set, the French took the lead with a score of six to five, but suddenly there was an error in the subjective opinion and it became six to six. But in the end, the French still won with a score of eight to six. As a result, Bolo Tala won three to two.

Kochland Wins the Old General 96

France has already won the fate of the singles championship after Du Lorat won. The nature of the competition between French Kochland and the old general Tielden is no different from a performance. Kochland was not without fatigue after two days of fierce battles, but his hitting skills were ingenious and he had complete control over others. From the completion of the second set, he showed his skills. The sudden killing was quick and timely, and Tielden became his victim. The American Tielden won the first set with the power of his shooting, but gradually became overwhelmed and it was difficult to preserve his innate skills. As a result, Kochland defeated the old general with a score of four to six, six to three, six to one, and seven to five.

School Equipment Exhibition Closed Yesterday 106

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's School Equipment Exhibition, held at Xicheng Meixi this time, displayed over 1,700 pieces of school equipment. The various tools are of considerable research value. It is heard that the bureau has hired various experts to classify and evaluate them. The evaluation methods are as follows: (1) The evaluation method will be based on the exhibition departments, and the scores will be calculated on a school basis. (2) The evaluation scoring items are as follows: Teaching, Moral Education, Child Psychology, Economy, Durability, Ease of Use, Exquisiteness, Creativity, Scope of Application, Inspiration. (3) For each of the above items, the best score is ten points. (4) The school's score statistics are as follows: 60-69 points: C; 70-89 points: B; 90-100 points: A. (5) The school's overall score is calculated by taking 30% of the total number of exhibits and 70% of the average quality of each item. (6) Critics of each department: School equipment: Fu Futian; Ordinary equipment: Ma Chonggan; Subject equipment: Xie Kang, Gong Jiaxin, Ding Chongxuan; Reference equipment: Ni Wenya; Entertainment equipment: Tang Shouqian. Each school can retrieve their exhibits today.

Record of the Unprecedented School Equipment Exhibition, Ms. Ye Hua 112

Our country's innovative education has been around for 32 years. Various exhibitions have been heard of. However, there has never been a school equipment exhibition because the scope of school equipment is too broad. Everything from children's clothing, food, shelter, and transportation to the school's living environment is school equipment. It is difficult to collect and even more difficult to exhibit. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, not fearing the trouble and annoyance, has opened an unprecedented school equipment exhibition at Xicheng and Meixi schools during this steaming hot summer season. How can this not be recorded? Therefore, a brief overview is recorded below.

▲Almost thought I was in the Rainbow Temple Lane. The Education Bureau held its first school equipment exhibition preparation meeting on February 19th. It has been more than 120 days since then. Now it is divided into five parts for display. The attendees and their quantities are: 28 schools with 218 pieces of ordinary equipment, 30 schools with 187 pieces of classroom equipment, 43 schools with 1,005 pieces of subject equipment, 24 schools with 279 pieces of entertainment equipment, and 9 schools with 76 pieces of reference items. Each department has unique and ingenious works. However, ordinary equipment is the most fascinating. Beds, chamber pots, tables, chairs, and stools are all available. It is as if selling a complete set of dowry. The spectators almost thought they were in the Rainbow Temple Lane in the world of dowry shops.

▲Bing Song Appreciates the Young Ladies and Wives. The opening ceremony of the exhibition invited He Bingsong, the chief editor of the Commercial Press and professor at Great China University, to give a lecture. He is a historian, and his talk did not deviate from his old profession. What are our country's school equipment? Historically, it has not been valued. Even the saying that teachers sit on cold benches is enough to imagine. Teachers' equipment is so bad, let alone students. When new education first started, only blackboards were set up but there was a lack of chalk. At that time, there was only borrowing from the face powder of young ladies and wives to write. Although teachers and students felt uncomfortable, they were grateful to the young ladies and wives for their unintentional help. Because if the young ladies and wives did not use face powder, such simple teaching equipment would still be difficult to appear.

▲The Teachers Act as Elementary School Students. On the first day, 356 elementary school teachers from the Education Bureau's summer school went to visit together from Xiaodongmen. Upon arrival, they must all sign in to distinguish diligence from laziness. After reading through it once, they unconsciously "felt the heat of the sun, sweat flowing, and their breath drooping and not recovering." So they gathered in the Xicheng auditorium to rest. The benches in the hall were low and small, originally intended for elementary school students. At this point, the teachers acted as elementary school students, sitting in rows, fanning and wiping sweat, laughing and talking. Among them, two or three fat people squatted in the center of the room, resembling Maitreya, feeling very contented. Visitors who saw it were amused.

Sea Goose in the Train 114

A few days ago, I went to Jin to visit my relatives. In the train from Beijing to Shanghai, I heard and saw a lot. Bored during the long day, I dipped my brush and recorded it. ▲Old Father Seeking Son An old man with a clear appearance sat in the corner, silent and sighing frequently. Looking at his attitude, he seemed to have something important on his mind. Everyone was surprised. Upon arriving in Suzhou, a gentleman in the same seat went forward and asked him. He said, "I am from Yuyao. I came to Jin to find my son. Three years ago, my son joined the army and was under Lord Hu's command. Recently, I heard that Lord Hu was defeated, and the wounded soldiers were transported back. Therefore, I went to Jin to find him." The gentleman said, "There are many wounded people. Can you find him?" The old man said, "I miss him very much. I don't know if he is safe or not. I am sixty years old and only have this one son." At that time, the old man's tears flowed uncontrollably, and he was extremely sad. Those sitting nearby could not help but wipe away their tears.

▲What is This? Two people wearing Zhongshan suits were talking loudly, as if there was no one else around. At first glance, they were officials. When the ticket inspector arrived, everyone presented their tickets for inspection. Only the two of them did not give their tickets. The ticket inspector asked them to buy tickets. They said sternly, "What is this?" and took out their badges. The ticket inspector thanked them.

▲Sweating Profusely About ten feet away from my seat were four weak women with wavy hair and rosy cheeks. They wore qipao and high-heeled shoes, extremely fashionable. When the train arrived in Wuxi, there was no cool breeze, and the heat was rising. They stuck their heads out of the window but still felt stuffy. The four women did not dare to move slightly, and the sweat poured down like rain. A student from a certain school laughed and said, "Today, I saw the true face of Mount Lu!" The four women glared at him.

▲Great Bad Luck. I like to eat biscuits. Even when it is hot, I can still eat them. What I brought with me that day was a basket of biscuits. When I was eating the biscuits, a child next to me was drooling and then started crying, asking his mother for them. I gave him a handful. His mother was furious and snatched it away, throwing it on the ground. I didn't understand why. The person sitting next to me was also surprised. All children want to eat when they see something. What was the purpose of snatching it away and throwing it on the ground? Was it because it was too little? To avoid suspicion? It's incomprehensible.

Eastern Travel Impressions (16), Qian Hua 116

(10) (3) Track and Field Stadium Layout

In recent years, our country's performance in various sports, especially track and field, has been the most disappointing. Since the Fifth Far Eastern Games, our country's situation has been deteriorating, and the opportunities to score points have been decreasing. At the Eighth Games held in Shanghai, we scored zero points. In this Games, we were fortunate to get one point, but in fact, it was because Japan's Nambu Chuhei did not participate in the triple jump. Nambu's performance is above Oda's. If he had entered the competition, Situ Guang would have been relegated to fifth place. Therefore, it was not really achieved through genuine ability. A certain person from the Japan Sports Association once told reporters that China's track and field performance can be said to have made very little progress. The Philippines progressed two steps, and Japan progressed four steps. In the future, no matter what, China and the Philippines will not be enemies of Japan. It is found that our country's track and field's lack of vitality and the audience's lack of interest are also major reasons. In sports meets in various places, ball games are always more crowded than track and field events. This is clear evidence. Therefore, how to attract the audience's interest is an issue that should be specially studied and remedied. What is recorded in this article can be used as a model for our countrymen, and people in the Sports Promotion Association should pay special attention to it. The reporter visited the Japanese National Track and Field Athletes Preliminary Selection Conference in Tokyo on May 16th and 17th. The layout of the track and field stadium was no different from the Far Eastern Games. The results of each competition were made very clear to the audience. In the Far Eastern Games, the reporter's job was very important, reporting the competition results at all times. News reporters did not have the trouble of running around for interviews, and the order of the meeting was very orderly. For example, in the 100-meter first group preliminary, the reporter reported the names of the participants and their running positions via radio before the event. A few minutes after the run, the results were reported, as well as the distance between the first and second place. The reporter seats were next to the reporter, so the information was clearer. They reported the news to the newspaper through desk telegraphs. Those without telephones wrote the results on small pieces of paper and sent them by carrier pigeons. In the meeting, printed order books were available, and the audience held a copy in their hands, listening quietly to the reporter's words and recording them one by one in the book. It was a scene of great joy. Tens of thousands of people in the field were actually performing the duties of reporters, so the interest was felt to be doubled. The equipment for the field events was even more thorough. For example, in the high jump and long jump, the reporter reported the names of the participants before the event. After each jump, the results were reported. When the six people selected in the preliminary were chosen, the names were reported again. After the competition, the results of the first to fourth place were reported in detail. Several wooden boards about several feet high were prepared in the field. The boards were black and had large white Arabic numerals written on them. For example, when the high jump reached a height of 1.95 meters, the wooden boards spelled out the numbers 195. It was very clear from a distance. For the discus and shot put, a white powder line was drawn to indicate a certain distance. For example, white lines were drawn for 30 meters, 35 meters, 40 meters, 45 meters, and 50 meters for the discus. Several small national flags were also prepared. When a Chinese athlete threw to a certain point, the Chinese flag was inserted there, fluttering in the wind. The distance of the throw and the distance compared to other countries were clear at a glance. At the Japanese National Preliminary Meeting, there was no distinction between countries, so these small flags were discarded and not used. Only a red small flag was inserted at the world record position to show the meaning of competition and encouragement. Therefore, the order of the field events was orderly. No one except the judges and athletes entered the field. Even photography reporters were severely restricted. Japanese newspapers are very quick to report sports news. The results of competitions before 3:30 PM can be published in the evening paper on the same day. Detailed manuscripts are available from the news agencies by 8:00 PM for news before 7:00 PM. This should also be attributed to the perfect layout of the track and field stadium. The order of our country's track and field stadium is the most chaotic. This has been the case in previous sports meets, and the last National Games in Hangzhou was even worse. The organizers issued judge badges indiscriminately, allowing people to enter the track and field to watch. Because the conference did not have an official report on the competition results, news reporters had no choice but to run around the field to interview. The reporter, Du Tingxiu, did not perform the duties of reporting and repeatedly declared on the radio that he was driving reporters out of the field, publicly insulting reporters, and exceeding the authority of the reporter. Reporters should not enter the field to interview, but the conference should order the reporter to report the results from time to time and maintain the order of the entire field indirectly. Therefore, the responsibility lies entirely with the improper conduct of the conference organizers. The lack of common sense of Du Tingxiu is especially laughable.

Recently, I have been interested in traveling and writing travel poems. I wonder if the two or three volumes of Sheng You Tu Yong have been published. I deeply yearn for them. Yimei and Xiumei are as gentle as good women, and their writing is brilliant. They are promising newcomers to the literary world. Zhian's poems are beautiful and elegant, and his opening lines startled the elders. However, Zhou Mengpo went to Mogan Mountain, and Zhao Banpo and Yan Zairu were ill. Sun Xueni and Tian Jihen said they would come but were hindered by affairs. They all replied in letters expressing their regret. Then, when the lights were brightly lit and the electric fans were blowing, just after entering the seat, the Western God arrived late and asked about Shou Juan. Hu Yishan also came late. The Yibu dishes were mostly named after delicacies, and everyone said they were delicious. The owner of the Reading Painting Building was a connoisseur, and Danlin liked to play with paintings by famous people. Since we had not seen each other for a long time, we talked at length during the banquet, planning to finely print the beauty and wealth of the art world that we had collected. Huahua heard this and rushed over, saying that amidst the ten-zhang red dust, during the hundred-degree photography season, a hall of elegant gatherings was full of celebrities. It was truly a way to spend the summer. Mr. Hu Jifan said that tonight's banquet was no different from the West Garden. Why not try to paint a picture? So I retreated and first drafted this record as the basis for making the picture. (No remuneration)

A Warm Feeling (2)(4)(3) Bao Tianxiao 117

Chapter 13: Who Plants Good Fortune Unintentionally Gains a Diamond Ring; Only This Fate Inspires a Song of Golden Threads

It turned out that the day the International Garden Fair was extended was also the day the Kindling Fortune lottery tickets were drawn in public. Many people bought a few tickets, as if they had already donated the money to others. Whether they won or not, they no longer paid attention. But there were also many ladies and young women who bought a ticket, harboring great hope. This was like the champagne tickets bought during the horse racing season, and before the drawing, it was as if the first prize was already in their pocket. Moreover, the first, second, and third prizes were all valuable treasures, so many people longed to win. In addition, the officers running the International Garden Fair were elated because the fair had been so successful. On the last day, they added many more amusements. In addition to Chinese and Western fireworks, there was also Western music and Chinese Kunqu opera singing, etc. As a result, the traffic was even busier than the previous three days. On that day, Shi Guanping was particularly excited. At three o'clock in the afternoon, he ran to the editorial office of the Ping Bao newspaper and said, "You should go to Zhang Garden. Today is the last day, and there are many more games and programs. And it is also the day when the Kindling Fortune tickets are drawn there. If you go, I have a carriage here." Everyone said, "It's enough to go once. The second time, it doesn't feel like anything special, just these little games. And going to a place like that always costs money. The food and drink in the fair are much more expensive than outside. You might even run into some familiar ladies and young women who will take advantage of you." Shi Guanping said, "I want to go and see. They gave me two hundred tickets. At first, I thought I wouldn't be able to get rid of them all. Later, you took five and I took ten, and I actually sold quite a few. Now I have less than twenty left. I think there must be some prizes among these two hundred tickets. Maybe not big prizes, but there must be a few small ones. After the lottery is drawn, the Kindling Fortune ticket organization will be finished. After I handle the winning tickets and distribute them, it will be none of my business." At this time, Zuo Shichen had just arrived at the newspaper office. Shi Guanping said to him, "How about it? Today is the public drawing for the Kindling Fortune tickets at Zhang Garden. Don't you have ten tickets too? Why not go and take a look together? Maybe the first prize is in your hands." Zuo Shichen said, "Okay, okay. If my ticket wins the first prize, please give me a call and let me know. I will come to collect the prize. Or please bring me the prize you collected." This was just a joke between the two, thinking that winning a big prize among so many tickets was like finding a needle in a haystack. Who knew that before four-thirty, Shi Guanping actually called from Wei Chun Garden and said to the tea boy, "Please ask Mr. Zuo to come and answer the phone." Zuo Shichen ran to answer it. Shi Guanping said, "Do you have your Kindling Fortune tickets with you?" Zuo Shichen searched all his pockets, but he didn't have them.

期麥突漲四五分 130

Wheat Futures Suddenly Rise Four to Five Points

中關麥廠胃漸活

The Central China Wheat Mills Gradually Become Active

Yesterday, the wheat futures market suddenly showed signs of tension after the opening bell, especially for July delivery. Although only three cars were involved, wheat from all over this year generally suffered from a common problem: the delivery coincided with the rainy season. The wheat harvested in various producing areas was generally considered to be of insufficient quality, and due to moisture and lack of proper sun drying, most of it was prone to heat damage, failing to meet the exchange's delivery standards. Therefore, people associated the scarcity of this month's delivery with future contracts, leading to a leap in prices for all months after the opening, rising by six to seven points compared to the previous week's closing price. In the afternoon, the market eased slightly as some long positions were unwound. As a result, August and September futures rose by five points each compared to the previous week, while October to December futures rose by four points each. The current wheat market condition is such that the mills are still active, and the high-quality wheat inventory is not large. Therefore, there is a gradual increase in activity in the Central China region, with prices in various grades increasing by two to three points. Over 8,000 bags of newly harvested and stored Shandong Yao Wan wheat and Nanjing wheat were purchased by Fuxin and Fufeng, it is said.

Silk and Tea – Unsuccessful Telegraphic Transfers Hinder Silk Sales

昨日本埠洋莊絲經交易依然清堅横濱日絲已見轉漲各歐莊對於期絲揑意雖濃而絲價不高華商絲本不敷加以昨日海外絲電不轉成交難暢昨祗信孚等進滬白廠經三十包開利進黄廠經二十包價均堅定云

Yesterday, the silk trade in foreign firms in this port remained stable and firm. Yokohama Japanese silk had already shown a price increase. European firms had a strong interest in silk futures, but the silk price was not high. Chinese silk was already in short supply, and yesterday's unsuccessful telegraphic transfers from overseas made transactions difficult. Yesterday, only Xinfu and others brought 30 bales of white filature silk to Shanghai, and Kaili brought 20 bales of yellow filature silk. Prices remained firm, it is said.

▲本廠布時屆七底疋頭商須墊銀者急謀走脫故不若前日之堅挺藍飛魚細布小去五分售七兩一錢七分半細斜亦小陽鶴售六兩九錢二分半藍雙魚六兩七錢藍雙魚細布因牛莊帮搜辦反漲二分半售六兩九錢七分半陽鶴六兩九錢半彩球同價粗布寗波帮採辦成交三百餘件九磅布現貨有殆盡之勢十一磅布亦漲二分半昨三兎·三鹿·人鐘一致須四兩七錢

▲東西疋東貨月華絨益形見硬執貨者均有不售之象第一功直貢缎小二厘半售二錢八分二厘半寳球細嗶嘰又跌湖心亭反硬毛絲布大跌均於二兩零五分售罄元直貢呢依然堅定三潭爲三錢一分半獵雁三錢零五厘莫干山三錢雙童鹿二錢六分冲素綢跌而復漲昨可愛美人洋藍·秃灰·札藍一致須四兩零五分西貨元羽綢長江帮略有成交泰西緞鎭江帮昨進十餘件云

五金英馬口鐵現貨軋缺 133

Hardware - British Tinplate Spot Market Extremely Short

英馬口鐵新近現貨十分蕭條各路客帮採辦甚力市貨有供不敷求之勢而標準飛黄騰達最近如蛋廠製罐廠之吸胃更見踴躍行情愈挺現價九十磅每箱價至十四兩二錢半一百磅十五兩四五錢聞連日市上開出共有八九百箱之多聞後批採辦者仍甚踴躍恐市上大有無貨以供買客之槪也

Recently, the spot market for British tinplate has been very sluggish. Various out-of-town merchants are actively purchasing, leading to a situation where supply cannot meet demand. The demand from standard brands such as Flying Yellow and Tengda, especially from egg factories and canning factories, is even more enthusiastic, further pushing up prices. The current price for 90-pound boxes is 14 taels, 2 mace, 5 fen per box, and 15 taels, 4 mace, 5 fen for 100-pound boxes. It is said that a total of 800 to 900 boxes have been sold in the market in recent days. It is also said that later batches of purchasers are still very enthusiastic, and there are fears that the market may run out of stock to supply buyers.

南北貨黑胡椒市盤大跌 134

North-South Goods - Black Pepper Market Plummets

同業議定公盤以維貨本

The Trade Association Agreed to a Public Offering to Maintain Capital

黑胡椒前因産價迭電報跌以致人心大起恐慌各行號欲圖爭脫手貨市盤一齊甩售故時僅三日自七十三兩之售盤暴跌至四十八兩半跌風之健實曩來所未有然各行號貨本均在六十兩以上兹特邀集同業議售公盤計定一號椒五十九兩黑大正牌五十八兩副牌五十七兩若有削價購售者一經查出即須儆罰期以兩月云云

Previously, due to repeated telegraphic reports of falling production prices for black pepper, people became greatly alarmed and panicked. Various firms tried to sell their goods as quickly as possible, leading to a massive sell-off in the market. In just three days, the selling price plummeted from 73 taels to 48.5 taels. Such a rapid decline has never been seen before. However, the cost basis for various firms is all above 60 taels. Therefore, the trade association was specially convened to sell through a public offering, with prices set at 59 taels for grade one pepper, 58 taels for the black Dazheng brand, and 57 taels for the secondary brand. Anyone found to be purchasing or selling at a reduced price will be punished, with a term of two months, etc.

昨日颶風來滬 136

Hurricane Hits Shanghai Yesterday

浦潮暴漲

The Huangpu River Swelled Rapidly

輪船停開

Ships Suspended Service

颶風吹入内海傾向我國江浙海面情形曾載昨報兹悉其中心點昨已進抵温州海面本埠大風亦已到臨行將出口之各海輪因得海關警告一律臨時受阻兹將詳情分紀如下

Yesterday's newspaper reported on the situation of a hurricane entering the inland sea and heading towards the coastal areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang in our country. We now know that its center had reached the Wenzhou sea yesterday. A strong wind has also arrived in this port. All ships about to leave the port were temporarily blocked due to customs warnings. The details are as follows:

▲本埠昨日大風本埠自前日起已有猛烈之東南風天空白雲趨向西北甚速似成風潮氣象入晚又有陣雨風亦轉大昨晨起其勢益烈因之日來酷熱暑氣爲之一消行路頗覺凉爽午後更猛浦中潮水因被風助暴漲數尺惟行駛船隻尙無危險

The Strong Wind in This Port Yesterday: Since the day before yesterday, this port has experienced a strong southeasterly wind. The white clouds in the sky moved towards the northwest very quickly, creating the appearance of a windstorm. There were also showers in the evening, and the wind also increased. From yesterday morning, its intensity increased. As a result, the recent intense heat and summer heat dissipated, and walking felt quite cool. In the afternoon, it became even stronger. The tide in the Huangpu River swelled rapidly by several feet due to the wind, but there was no danger to the ships sailing.

▲颶風進抵海岸前在太平洋上向西北方猛進之新颶颼自吹入内海後繼續向西北迅速進發昨日午後四時據洋涇浜天文台報告颶風之中心區域已過大海吹抵福州與温州間之海岸正在登陸云云惟昨日本埠所到之大風尙在颶風中心點之外者則中心風力之鉅可知且天文台報告力量較上次確爲猛烈大致浙海省海岸已將成災云

Before the Hurricane Reached the Coast: The new hurricane, which was advancing vigorously in a northwest direction in the Pacific Ocean, continued to advance rapidly in a northwest direction after blowing into the inland sea. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the Yangjingbang Observatory reported that the central area of the hurricane had crossed the sea and reached the coast between Fuzhou and Wenzhou, where it was making landfall, etc. However, the strong wind that reached this port yesterday was still outside the center of the hurricane, so the magnitude of the central wind force can be known. Moreover, the observatory reported that the force was indeed more violent than the last time. It is likely that the coast of Zhejiang Province will be devastated.

▲海關鳴砲警告浦東陸家嘴海關旗台因據天文台報告颶風已抵温州海岸故於昨日午後四時半特高懸黑色警球同時開放警砲一響警告各海輪一律不可出口以避危險

Customs Fired Warning Cannon: The Customs flag station at Lujiazui in Pudong, based on the observatory's report that the hurricane had reached the coast of Wenzhou, specially hoisted a black warning ball at 4:30 PM yesterday and fired a warning cannon to warn all ships that they must not leave the port to avoid danger.

▲天文台昨晚警告徐家匯天文台昨晚九時特别警告云颶風吹至温州附近海岸其勢甚猛方向爲東北·北因欲折經陸地吹向此間而來致進行遲緩吳淞口外海面波浪洶湧

The Observatory Warned Last Night: The Xujiahui Observatory issued a special warning at 9:00 PM last night, saying that the hurricane had blown to the coast near Wenzhou and was very strong. The direction was northeast-north. Because it wanted to turn and blow here via land, its progress was slow. The sea outside the Wusongkou was turbulent.

▲滬甬班輪停開太古新北京寗紹新寗紹昨爲赴甬正班船期在下午四時以前尙裝載客貨出售船票準備出口及至得海關警砲遂停收貨件並將已售船票退回各客一面通知各旅客聲明因避風停航一班搭客退離上岸者約有千餘名之多該二船昨未駛出

The Shanghai-Ningbo Liners Suspended Service: Taikoo's Xin Beijing and Ningshao's Xin Ningshao were scheduled to depart for Ningbo yesterday. Before 4:00 PM, they were still loading passengers and cargo, selling tickets, and preparing to leave the port. When they heard the customs cannon, they stopped receiving cargo and refunded the tickets that had been sold. They notified the passengers, stating that the voyage was suspended to avoid the storm. About a thousand passengers disembarked and went ashore. The two ships did not depart yesterday.

▲來船中途避風招商局温州班海晏輪行至台州因海面發生颶風電滬在該處避風展延進口期一天怡和之廣生輪昨日亦在吳淞外途中抛泊避風未及來滬又有舟山公司之舟山輪由台州來滬亦停抛在途以避颶風故昨日進口船甚少

Ships Avoiding the Storm En Route: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyan, which was en route to Wenzhou, sent a telegram to Shanghai stating that it was avoiding the storm in Taizhou due to a hurricane on the sea, extending the import period by one day. Jardine Matheson's Guangsheng also anchored to avoid the storm en route outside Wusong yesterday and was unable to reach Shanghai. In addition, the Zhoushan Company's Zhoushan, which was en route from Taizhou to Shanghai, also stopped and anchored en route to avoid the hurricane. Therefore, very few ships arrived yesterday.

▲出口海輪延期沿海輪船之展期開行者尙有三北之萬象招商之嘉禾均往福州因大風而延遲一天出口尙有東港公司之升利輪昨晚亦未開出須今日赴象山也其他已經離滬之海輪多抛吳淞口外守候風息後再行

Export Ships Postponed: Among the coastal ships that postponed their departure, there are still Sanbei's Wanxiang and China Merchants' Jiahe, both heading to Fuzhou, which were delayed by one day due to the strong wind. Donggang Company's Shengli also did not depart last night and must go to Xiangshan today. Other ships that had already left Shanghai mostly anchored outside the Wusongkou, waiting for the wind to subside before continuing.

▲大華輪船微損平安公司之大華輪自台州來滬昨日進口時因風大潮激其船身在浦江抛停之時爲風浪衝激而致撞損當時不能開行即將來貨卸清後略予修理改延至今日開班

The Dahua Steamer Suffered Slight Damage: The Ping An Company's Dahua, which was en route from Taizhou to Shanghai, was damaged yesterday when it was entering the port due to the strong wind and tidal surge. When its hull was anchored in the Huangpu River, it was impacted by the wind and waves, causing damage. At that time, it could not sail, so the goods were unloaded and slightly repaired, and the departure was postponed to today.

王伯羣之談話 137

Wang Boqun's Speech

收回電話權交涉

Negotiations to Reclaim Telephone Rights

中美航空權問題

The Issue of Sino-American Aviation Rights

平津間郵務工潮

The Postal Workers' Strike Between Peiping (Beijing) and Tientsin (Tianjin)

中日電信交涉正在進行昨日外王已與重光作初步之接治將來由交部負責與日方接洽交涉收回查中日電信水綫有三一由上海至長崎二由青島至佐世保三爲東北南滿鐵路之電信權均在二月份次第期滿本報記者昨晤交長王伯羣氏時曾詢及此事及其他問題兹將王氏所談分述如次

The Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations are in progress. Yesterday, Foreign Minister Wang had a preliminary meeting with Shigemitsu. In the future, the Ministry of Communications will be responsible for contacting the Japanese side to negotiate the recovery. It is found that there are three Sino-Japanese telecommunications submarine cables: one from Shanghai to Nagasaki, one from Qingdao to Sasebo, and the third is the telecommunications rights of the Northeast South Manchuria Railway, all of which will expire in February. When our newspaper reporter met with Minister of Communications Wang Boqun yesterday, he inquired about this matter and other issues. Minister Wang's statements are summarized as follows:

▲收回電信權王氏謂關於收回電信權交涉如大東大北及中日水綫等均在範圍以内按日本對於電信權絶對屬於國有不許其他任何機關獲有營業權但法國則反是可以自由經營交部方針擬用日本政策最低限度對於其營業權亦須加以相當限制庶政府可以操持監督

Reclaiming Telecommunications Rights: Minister Wang said that negotiations on reclaiming telecommunications rights, such as the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Sino-Japanese submarine cables, are all within the scope. According to Japan, telecommunications rights are absolutely owned by the state, and no other organization is allowed to obtain operating rights. However, France, on the contrary, can freely operate. The Ministry of Communications plans to use the Japanese policy, and at a minimum, impose considerable restrictions on their operating rights so that the government can maintain control and supervision.

▲三月後進行現時因眞茹大電臺尙未建築工竣加以金潮高漲遽言收回我國吃虧過大太不合算且市上公債種類已多再有發行定感困難故交部現時對日丹各方頗願加以研究討論詳爲接洽至備價收回俟二月後大電臺告成再開始積極進行屆時金價亦可望稍跌

Proceeding After March: Currently, because the construction of the Zhenru Grand Radio Station has not been completed, coupled with the rising gold tide, it would be too disadvantageous and not cost-effective to hastily say that we will reclaim it. Moreover, there are already many types of government bonds on the market, and it will definitely be difficult to issue more. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications is currently very willing to conduct research and discussion with Japan and Denmark to negotiate in detail. As for the preparation for repurchase, we will start actively after the Grand Radio Station is completed after February. At that time, the gold price is also expected to fall slightly.

▲新公司成立王氏又謂關於中美航空問題現合同已簽字資本我百分五十五美飛運公司百分四十五董事我三美二各種用人行政均按資本分配曾開過董事會二次新公司已完全成立但仍沿用中國航空公司名義

Establishment of a New Company: Minister Wang also said that regarding the Sino-American aviation issue, the contract has been signed. Our capital is 55%, and the American Flying Transport Company's is 45%. The board of directors consists of three Chinese and two Americans. All personnel and administration are allocated according to capital. The board of directors has been convened twice, and the new company has been fully established, but it will still use the name of China National Aviation Corporation.

▲我國資本金我國資本金由滬蓉航空處及前中國航空公司資産撥入計共作價爲四百萬元尙短少百五十萬元美方資本已足我國所短少之資金仍由交行擔保美方亦已承認至前滬蓉之技術人員已盡量介紹至新公司服務

Our Capital: Our capital is allocated from the assets of the Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Office and the former China National Aviation Corporation, totaling 4 million yuan. There is still a shortage of 1.5 million yuan. The American capital is sufficient. The funds that our country is short of are still guaranteed by the Bank of Communications, which has also been recognized by the American side. As for the technical personnel of the former Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Office, they have been introduced to the new company as much as possible.

▲平津郵工潮記者詢以處理平津郵務工潮辦法王氏謂當由北平郵務局負責辦理交部以不累及民衆爲主旨近日北來郵件多不貼郵票照章應由受主倍罰但爲體恤計曾令郵局不必施罚僅補足原價爲止云云又王氏近稍感不適暫時養疴滬上並不返京

The Postal Workers' Strike in Peiping (Beijing) and Tientsin (Tianjin): When the reporter asked about the method of handling the postal workers' strike in Peiping (Beijing) and Tientsin (Tianjin), Minister Wang said that the Peiping (Beijing) Postal Bureau should be responsible for handling it. The Ministry of Communications aims not to burden the public. Recently, many letters from the north do not have postage stamps. According to the regulations, the recipient should be fined double the amount. However, out of consideration for the people, the post office has been ordered not to impose fines, but only to make up the original price, etc. Also, Minister Wang has recently felt slightly unwell and is temporarily recuperating in Shanghai and will not return to Beijing.

王伯羣派蔡致平維持招商局務 138

Wang Boqun Dispatches Cai Zhiping to Maintain the Affairs of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

並呈國府速委專員負責

And Submits a Request to the National Government to Appoint a Commissioner to be Responsible as Soon as Possible

交部主張將來官商合辦

The Ministry of Communications Advocates Joint Government-Private Operation in the Future

本報記者昨日下午訪晤交通部長王伯羣氏詢以招商局之善後問題據云余已於昨晚（即二十七日）電交部派航政司長蔡致平暫爲維持招商局務一方面呈請國府速派專員正式負責辦理一切至招商局組織問題前次交部及工商部曾會呈中常會主張官商合辦由政府撥資本若干作爲股欵然後較易整理但中委陳立夫氏則主由政府收回此案至今懸而未决預料將來俟中常會决定方針後則招商局根本問題解决餘事均可迎刃而解云云

Yesterday afternoon, our newspaper reporter interviewed Minister of Communications Wang Boqun to inquire about the aftermath of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. According to him, I telegraphed the Ministry of Communications last night (i.e., the 27th) to dispatch Cai Zhiping, Director of the Department of Navigation Affairs, to temporarily maintain the affairs of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. On the one hand, I submitted a request to the National Government to appoint a commissioner to be formally responsible for handling everything. As for the organizational problem of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce had previously jointly submitted a proposal to the Central Standing Committee advocating joint government-private operation, with the government allocating some capital as shares, which would make it easier to reorganize. However, Central Committee member Chen Lifu advocated that the government take it back. This case is still pending. It is expected that in the future, after the Central Standing Committee decides on the policy, the fundamental problem of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be resolved, and all other matters can be easily solved, etc.

重光葵昨謁外王 139

Shigemitsu Aoi Visited Foreign Minister Wang Yesterday

商談中日電信交涉

To Discuss the Sino-Japanese Telecommunications Negotiations

秋凉後再晋京續商

To Resume Negotiations in Beijing After the Autumn Cools Down

王正廷昨下午返京

Wang Zhengting Returned to Beijing Yesterday Afternoon

He plans to go to Beijing after the autumn cools down to start consultations with the Ministry of Communications. Shigemitsu did not mention the issue of Arita's ambassadorship to China, etc. Wang returned to Beijing by car at 2:45 PM yesterday afternoon.
