Book and Newspaper Introductions 184

An Overview of Chinese Folk Literature (Continued) Written by Yang Yin Shen

Chapter Two, "Folk Literature and Literature," systematically describes the value of folk literature and what is commonly referred to as literature, as well as their relationship and differences, so that we have a deeper understanding of folk literature. According to the author's observations, there is no significant difference between the value of folk literature and what is commonly referred to as literature. That is to say, they are one and two, two and one. At the same time, they have a close relationship because many aspects of literature rely on folk literature. This is the inherent noble position of folk literature.

Literature is evolving. Therefore, the first thing that emerged was poetry, which also evolved from the songs of primitive peoples. This is described very clearly and thoroughly in this chapter, and it cites the formation of ancient Greek literary odes and epics, which are closely related to the myths and legends of their time and even draw material from them. This makes the argument of this book more explicit, and readers can certainly believe it without a doubt.

According to the author's research, there are four differences between folk literature and literary literature in terms of nature and form. First, oral vs. written. Second, mass vs. individual. Third, common vs. aristocratic. Fourth, natural vs. embellished. The arguments are mostly based on objective facts, and I don't need to explain them further, because looking at these four subheadings can reveal something of them. From these points of view, folk literature actually surpasses literary literature in some respects.

Chapter Three, "The Origin of Folk Literature," describes how folk literature came into being and why it came into being. The so-called folk literature came into being, and how did folk literature evolve and why did folk literature permanently exist among the people? The author has expounded on all these kinds of questions.

In fact, before "literature flourished," there was already folk literature "passed down by word of mouth." The emergence of literature is nothing more than "emotion moving within and taking shape in words." The formation of folk literature certainly cannot escape this example. Literature originates from poetry, and poetry originates from songs. These songs are generally the earliest form of folk literature. Their themes are mostly related to gods, and thus "mythology" was produced. Other forms such as "legends," "fables," "ballads," "riddles," "current tunes," etc., were mostly influenced by foreign "Buddhist music" and the promotion of literary literature. This chapter explores the relationship between literature and life in detail.

Chapter Four, "The Value of Folk Literature." The value described here is explored from another perspective, because it has already been said that its position in literature is equal to that of literary literature, and it even tends to surpass it. First, it can serve as "supplement to high education." Second, it can serve as "academic reference." Third, it can serve as "administrative basis." Fourth, it can serve as "life adjustment." The arguments are insightful and make us understand that folk literature not only has considerable value in itself, but also occupies many important positions in other aspects.

Of course, we should clarify the scope of folk literature. In Chapter Five, "Classification of Folk Literature," the author uses keen eyes and correct goals to identify the categories that truly belong to folk literature, for example:

The first category, "stories," can be divided into four types: 1. Myths ("stories containing religious elements"); 2. Legends ("stories containing historical elements"); 3. Anecdotes ("stories containing humorous elements"); 4. Fables ("stories containing satirical elements").

The second category, "songs," is also divided into four types: 1. Nursery rhymes ("songs sung by children"); 2. Mountain songs ("songs sung by adults"); 3. Current tunes ("general songs with chapters and melodies"); 4. Riddles ("general songs with hidden meanings"). The third category, "scripts," is only divided into two types: 1. Lyrics ("scripts with singing but no acting"); 2. Opera ("scripts with singing and acting").

Whether the author's classification is appropriate is not something we should judge strongly, but at least it can give readers a systematic concept. At the same time, Chapter Six, "Works of Folk Literature," is based on the above classification and cites relevant works. If we read it in reference to the above, it will be easier to understand. In each excerpt, the author provides detailed, objective descriptions and explanations. Therefore, this chapter occupies three-quarters of the entire book. The distribution of quantity is inevitably uneven. This seems to be the only drawback of this book.

Although this book is named "An Overview," the Chinese literati have always neglected folk literature. Now, it is possible to discover such a systematic book that studies this type of literature, which is really worthy of our attention. This is like gold mixed with yellow mud, and someone has spared valuable time and energy to excavate it. How much is obtained and whether "gold" can be scooped up is, of course, another question. However, the work that the author is currently implementing is worthy of our praise and should be paid attention to, because it provides a considerable indication for those who study or love folk literature and can also serve as a reference.

What China has is nothing more than a collection of some folk literature. As for books on this kind of research, I am afraid that Mr. Yang's book is the first of its kind. This point alone is enough for me to introduce it here.

Works of Chen Qiuzhang of the White Goose Painting Society

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introductions 185

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all books and newspapers on politics, economics, law, science, education, etc. are included in the introduction. However, frivolous books will not be introduced.

Drawings are limited to recent works by new artists at home and abroad and illustrations related to the text.

(2) Manuscripts on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(3) Drawings and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(4) Each text should not exceed 3,000 words.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally or in a sloppy manner. Western text can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translated text.

(7) Do not use blue ink for drawings attached to the manuscript, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black ink.

(8) Please indicate that the manuscript is received by the Book and Newspaper Introduction Department.

(9) Manuscripts will not be returned regardless of whether they are published or not. If they need to be returned, please declare in advance and attach sufficient postage.

(10) Remuneration for text is divided into three types: four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan per thousand words. Remuneration for drawings and photos is the same as above. Special manuscripts will be calculated separately.

Market News 186

The Sincere Company on Nanjing Road and Tianjin Road and the Yude Pool declare that since the pool was taken over by the giant merchant Yang Shunquan last year, its business has been booming. The internal manager, Fang Daoquan, has considerable social skills. To celebrate its anniversary, from August 2, gifts will be given and a type of 20% discount neighborhood coupon will be sold, which can be used all year round. This preferential treatment for customers is a unique approach in the bathroom industry. A grand occasion is expected at that time.

The Miaoji Department Store on North Sichuan Road declares that its ninth anniversary grand sale and prize giveaway will expire at 10 pm on the 31st of this month. After the expiry date, it will definitely not be extended. Counting from today, there are only three days left. The lottery will be held at the company at 9 am on August 1. In addition to reporters being present to monitor the event, all sectors are welcome to visit.

The Huiluo Company on Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road declares that it is the oldest and most reputable department store in Shanghai. It has a cheap one-yuan sale every month and a large winter and summer sale every year. The cheap one-yuan sale only includes parts, old stock, and paintings at one yuan. Other famous and valuable items are not discounted. However, all goods in all departments, whether in stock or new, must be sold at a discount during the winter and summer sales. This summer sale is scheduled to begin next week. All goods have been marked with low prices, especially the women's clothing department, where prices are the most suitable. New fabrics are piled up like mountains, which is breathtaking. At a time when gold is expensive and silver is cheap and prices are soaring, this large-scale sale at such a cheap price is bound to cause a sensation throughout Shanghai. In addition, this large sale will last for one month.

Hanli Company declares that printing equipment in our country has always been old-fashioned, either bulky and difficult to move or complicated to operate. Stencil duplicators come from our eastern neighbors, and the fonts they print are not beautiful. The other various printing tools and paper are few and can only print various floating forms. They cannot print documents that can be permanently retained. The Zhongling pneumatic press has the advantages of clear printing and various printing equipment. It is simple and quick enough to defeat stencil duplicators. At a time when the wave of advocating domestic goods is sweeping the country, our company has emerged with the latest inventions to meet the needs. All sectors are happy to use and promote it without reservation. Government dignitaries have especially praised it. Recently, Song Ziwen, Minister of Finance of the National Government, inscribed a praise: "Inscribed for the Zhongling Printing Machine, the ingenious machine is ingeniously developed and the patterns are new. It has made great contributions to culture and has also recovered rights and interests. How can it be compared to the ingenuity of ordinary machinery?" The inscription ends with Song Ziwen.

The Xu Chongdao Pharmacy declares that it is a giant in the national pharmaceutical industry in Shanghai and has a very long history since its establishment. Due to the development of its business, there are now eight branches and two affiliated branches. The eighth branch has recently opened and is located at the eastern end of Meibaige Road, Jing'an Temple Road. The transportation is convenient, and the location is ideal. Customers are showing great interest. The goods are especially conscientious. The head office and branches specialize in ginseng, bird's nest, and other precious tonics and beverage medicinal materials. At this time of hot summer, summer medicines are on the market, such as Bixun Dan, Xingjun San, and Shiqi Pills, which are all available. Recently, a new all-purpose Shiyao Water has been invented, which is refined with steam using scientific methods. Various floral dew are cooling, appetizing, epidemic prevention, and heatstroke prevention. Sales are very strong, so the staff of the head office and branches have been extremely busy in recent days.

The Hezong Oil Company declares that the American California Union Oil Company has sent a delegation to China to allocate 20 million gold yuan to establish a branch in China to promote the company's products. The delegation has already taken a chartered plane from Shanghai yesterday (the 22nd) to Nanjing, Jiujiang, Yichang, Hankou, and other ports to conduct on-site surveys of all business conditions. The company will use a letter to introduce the delegation to visit various agencies and authorities in various places.

The Guanmei Hat Factory on North Sichuan Road declares that the Taintan brand straw hats and felt hats produced by the factory since its opening have been popular throughout the country and as far as the South Seas Islands. The quality is excellent and the styles are new and unique, and it has long been widely praised. At this time when gold is expensive and silver is cheap, it is a good opportunity to promote domestic goods. In view of this, the factory has specially prepared a large number of felt hats to put on the market. The quality and style are far better than imported ones, and the prices are exceptionally low. This is a good message for promoting domestic goods.

The programs are all rare and unheard of by people at sea, such as the destruction of beautiful women in the middle of the body, the Hong Kong illusion, and the magic box, which are now performed by Nicola in the summer. Zhang also has all of the divine skills that were thought to be unique to Nicola. As for other large programs, all of them are the crystallization of Zhang's personal thoughts, which are far beyond what ordinary magicians can achieve, and all of them will be performed at the same time.
